319 namespace
320 {
321 
322 DepthwiseConvolution2dDescriptor MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(uint32_t strideX, uint32_t strideY,
323  uint32_t depthMultiplier = 1, uint32_t padLeft = 0, uint32_t padRight = 0,
324  uint32_t padTop = 0, uint32_t padBottom = 0)
325 {
326  IgnoreUnused(depthMultiplier);
327 
328  DepthwiseConvolution2dDescriptor desc;
329 
330  desc.m_PadLeft = padLeft;
331  desc.m_PadRight = padRight;
332 
333  desc.m_PadTop = padTop;
334  desc.m_PadBottom = padBottom;
335  desc.m_StrideX = strideX;
336  desc.m_StrideY = strideY;
337  desc.m_BiasEnabled = false;
338 
339  return desc;
340 }
341 
342 TensorInfo CreateOutputTensorInfo(const TensorInfo& inputInfo,
343  const TensorInfo& weightsInfo,
344  const DepthwiseConvolution2dDescriptor& descriptor,
345  DataType dataType)
346 {
347  const TensorShape& inputShape = inputInfo.GetShape();
348  const TensorShape& filterShape = weightsInfo.GetShape();
349 
350  unsigned int inWidth = inputShape[3];
351  unsigned int inHeight = inputShape[2];
352  unsigned int inBatchSize = inputShape[0];
353 
354  unsigned int filterWidth = filterShape[2];
355  unsigned int readWidth = (inWidth + descriptor.m_PadLeft + descriptor.m_PadRight) - (filterWidth);
356  unsigned int outWidth = 1u + (readWidth / descriptor.m_StrideX);
357 
358  unsigned int filterHeight = filterShape[1];
359  unsigned int readHeight = (inHeight + descriptor.m_PadTop + descriptor.m_PadBottom) - (filterHeight);
360  unsigned int outHeight = 1u + (readHeight / descriptor.m_StrideY);
361 
362  unsigned int outChannels = filterShape[3];
363  unsigned int outBatchSize = inBatchSize;
364 
365  TensorShape outputShape({outBatchSize, outChannels, outHeight, outWidth});
366  return TensorInfo(outputShape, dataType);
367 }
368 }
369 
370 TEST_CASE("DepthwiseConv2dUtils")
371 {
372  const DataType dataType = DataType::Float32;
373 
374  TensorInfo inputInfo({1, 1, 10, 10 }, dataType);
375  TensorInfo outputInfo;
376  TensorInfo weightsInfo3x3({ 1, 3, 3, 1 }, dataType, 0, 0, true); // [1,H,W,I*M]
377  TensorInfo biasesInfo;
378 
379  DepthwiseConvolution2dDescriptor descriptor;
380  NeonLayerSupport layerSupport;
381 
382  // Strides supported: 1,2,3
383  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(1, 1);
384  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
385  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
386  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
387 
388  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(1, 2);
389  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
390  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
391  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
392 
393  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(1, 3);
394  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
395  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
396  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
397 
398  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(2, 1);
399  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
400  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
401  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
402 
403  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(2, 2);
404  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
405  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
406  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
407 
408  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(2, 3);
409  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
410  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
411  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
412 
413  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(3, 1);
414  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
415  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
416  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
417 
418  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(3, 2);
419  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
420  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
421  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
422 
423  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(3, 3);
424  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
425  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
426  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
427 
428  // Supported stride 4
429  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(4, 1);
430  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
431  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
432  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
433 
434  // Supported weights shape 1x1
435  TensorInfo weightsInfo1x1({ 1, 1, 1, 1 }, DataType::Float32, 0, 0, true);
436  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(1, 1);
437  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo1x1, descriptor, dataType);
438  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
439  weightsInfo1x1, biasesInfo));
440 
441  // Supported shape 2x2
442  TensorInfo weightsInfo2x2({ 1, 2, 2, 1 }, DataType::Float32, 0, 0, true);
443  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(1, 1);
444  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo2x2, descriptor, dataType);
445  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
446  weightsInfo2x2, biasesInfo));
447 
448  // Asymmetric padding
449  descriptor = MakeDepthwiseConv2dDesc(1, 1, 1, 1, 2, 1, 2);
450  outputInfo = CreateOutputTensorInfo(inputInfo, weightsInfo3x3, descriptor, dataType);
451  CHECK(layerSupport.IsDepthwiseConvolutionSupported(inputInfo, outputInfo, descriptor,
452  weightsInfo3x3, biasesInfo));
453 }
